srcset="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"></div><!-- .featured-image -->\n\n\t<header class="entry-header">\n\t<div class="entry-header-row">\n\t\t<div class="entry-header-column">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class="entry-meta">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class="cat-links">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href="https://patriots4truth.org/category/history/" rel="category tag">History</a>\t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<span class="posted-on"><a href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/05/31/dropping-historic-a-bombs/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-05-31T17:47:55+00:00">May 31, 2022</time><time class="updated" datetime="2022-05-31T23:38:50+00:00">May 31, 2022</time></a></span>\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<a href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/05/31/dropping-historic-a-bombs/" rel="permalink"><h1 class="entry-title">Dropping Historic A-Bombs</h1></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-header-column -->\n\t</div><!-- .entry-header-row -->\n</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class="entry-content">\n\t\n<p><strong>USS <em>Augusta</em> (CL/CA-31)</strong> was a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northampton-class_cruiser"><em>Northampton</em>-class</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cruiser">cruiser</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Navy">United States Navy</a>, notable for service as a headquarters ship during <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Torch">Operation Torch</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Overlord">Operation Overlord</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Dragoon">Operation Dragoon</a>, and for her occasional use as a presidential flagship carrying both <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_S._Truman">Harry S. Truman</a> under wartime conditions (including at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlantic_Charter">Atlantic Charter</a>). (Wiki <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Augusta_(CA-31)">Source</a>)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Did you know that Harry Truman met on the Augusta (in international waters, just off the coast of England) with King George VI. Winston Churchill would have accompanied King George on such a high-level meeting, but we have not yet found source material regarding this. </p>\n\n\n\n<h3>On August 2, 1945 </h3>\n\n\n\n<h3><a href="https://www.trumanlibrary.gov/photograph-records/64-372-01">King George VI and President Harry S. Truman met aboard the USS Augusta</a></h3>\n\n\n\n<h3><a href="https://www.trumanlibrary.gov/photograph-records/63-1378-26">King George VI&#8217;s Barge Travels to the USS Augusta</a></h3>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img data-attachment-id="10164" /></noscript></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>On August 6, 1945, during World War II,  an American B-29 bomber dropped the world\xe2\x80\x99s first deployed atomic bomb over the Japanese city of Hiroshima.</strong> The explosion immediately killed an estimated 80,000 people; tens of thousands more would later die of radiation exposure. Three days later, a second B-29 dropped another A-bomb on Nagasaki, killing an estimated 40,000 people. Japan\xe2\x80\x99s Emperor Hirohito announced his country\xe2\x80\x99s unconditional surrender in World War II in a radio address on August 15, citing the devastating power of \xe2\x80\x9ca new and most cruel bomb.\xe2\x80\x9d (<a href="https://www.history.com/topics/world-war-ii/bombing-of-hiroshima-and-nagasaki">Source</a>)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>On 2 August, she embarked her distinguished passengers again, and received another visit from King&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_VI_of_the_United_Kingdom" target="_blank">George VI</a>.&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Truman" target="_blank">Harry Truman</a>&nbsp;was on the ship when he got the news that&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiroshima" target="_blank">Hiroshima</a>&nbsp;had been bombed by an atomic bomb. (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Augusta_(CA-31)#Normandy">Source</a>)</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Inquiring minds&#8230;. want to know. </em></p>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-image size-large srcset="https://i0.wp.com/patriots4truth.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/question-mark.png?resize=868%2C1024&amp;ssl=1 868w, /></noscript></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Was Truman getting permission to bomb Hiroshima and Nagasaki from the British Monarch (Pilgrims) headed by King George VI? Why was the King meeting with Truman when Winston Churchill was Truman&#8217;s political equivalent. What was the Monarch&#8217;s (Pilgrim&#8217;s) role in the bombing of Japan?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Was Winston Churchill, the father of WWII, Truman&#8217;s handler for the Pilgrims?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Were there two nuclear bombs dropped, or were they just more firebombings that had annihilated dozens of Japanese cities? </p>\n\n\n\n<h3><em>Flash forward &#8211; will Joe Biden have to ask permission from <a href="https://aim4truth.org/2021/01/22/breaking-the-white-house-has-been-stolen-by-the-british-this-is-the-war-of-1812-v-2-0/">Sir Nigel Knowles</a> to bomb Russia? </em></h3>\n\n\n\n<div style="height:89px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>\n\n\n\n<h2>You know who else was on the USS Augusta that day?</h2>\n\n\n\n<div style="height:31px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img src="https://i0.wp.com/aim4truth.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/Robert-Torba-war-record-1024x512.jpg?resize=845%2C423&#038;ssl=1" alt class="wp-image-141040 jetpack-lazy-image" data-recalc-dims="1" data-lazy-src="https://i0.wp.com/aim4truth.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/Robert-Torba-war-record-1024x512.jpg?resize=845%2C423&amp;is-pending-load=1#038;ssl=1" srcset="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"><noscript><img data-lazy-fallback="1" src="https://i0.wp.com/aim4truth.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/Robert-Torba-war-record-1024x512.jpg?resize=845%2C423&#038;ssl=1" alt="" class="wp-image-141040" data-recalc-dims="1" /></noscript></figure>\n\n\n\n<p><a href="https://fbcoverup.com/docs/library/1950-04-11-Robert-Thomas-Torba-Application-for-World-War-II-Compensation-Serv-No-9217099-Form-No-1-No-41921-Batch-Control-No-32187-Pennsylvania-WWII-Veterans-Bureau-Apr-11-1950.pdf" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Robert Thomas Torba. Pennsylvania WWII Veterans Bureau.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Torba\xe2\x80\x99s grandfather was \xe2\x80\x9cRobert Thomas Torba.\xe2\x80\x9d who served in the US Navy on the TOP SECRET USS Augusta &nbsp;Sep. 23, href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/05/26/the-andrew-torba-problem-of-stolen-technology/" rel="permalink"><h1 class="entry-title">Andrew Torba&#8217;s Problem of Gab&#8217;s Stolen Technology</h1></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-header-column -->\n\t</div><!-- .entry-header-row -->\n</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class="entry-content">\n\t\n<p>By Tyla</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Many of you ask why I beat up on platforms and people like Andrew Torba for using STOLEN TECHNOLOGY as the foundation for their social media networking platforms.</strong> Briefly, here&#8217;s my backstory.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Back in 2010, as the use of social networking was gaining more popularity in the school community (I have been in the education biz since the early 90s), I was concerned about the safety and security of using platforms like Facebook to conduct school online conversations and picture-postings of children. I decided to try my hand at it. I raised $100k in grant money to develop a school-centered social media platform. Of course, in hindsight, I see that I was quite naive about the corruption in social networking. </p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>We called the project Mudpies and Butterflies. Here are two promo videos still available on YouTube. </strong></p>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-4-3 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">\n<span class="embed-youtube" style="text-align:center; display: block;"><iframe loading="lazy" class="youtube-player" width="845" height="476" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/TvGoIJBsswI?version=3&#038;rel=1&#038;showsearch=0&#038;showinfo=1&#038;iv_load_policy=1&#038;fs=1&#038;hl=en-US&#038;autohide=2&#038;wmode=transparent" allowfullscreen="true" style="border:0;" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-presentation"></iframe></span>\n</div></figure>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">\n<span class="embed-youtube" style="text-align:center; display: block;"><iframe loading="lazy" class="youtube-player" width="845" height="476" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Tq0ztqcLKcc?version=3&#038;rel=1&#038;showsearch=0&#038;showinfo=1&#038;iv_load_policy=1&#038;fs=1&#038;hl=en-US&#038;autohide=2&#038;wmode=transparent" allowfullscreen="true" style="border:0;" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-presentation"></iframe></span>\n</div></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>As the project was being completed, I required the IT developer to secure all the licenses we needed so that our site was legit. However, there was one license that the technical team could not resolve: The foundational platform that all social media networks are placed on. They couldn&#8217;t find the original license holder. In the end, I was told that IBM developed the platform and that they had given it as OPEN SOURCE so that everyone could use it for free. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>NO WAY! I told the technicians that IBM NEVER gives anything away for free. I told them that if we couldn&#8217;t secure proper licenses from IBM, we could no longer continue the project because at any time IBM could close our site down. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So the project was shelved&#8230; but my inquisitive mind never stopped asking why this product was given out for FREE. This was the early beginnings for my search for TRUTH about IBM and social media.</p>\n\n\n<div class="wp-block-image">\n<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img data-attachment-id="107" /></noscript></figure>\n\n\n\n<h3>Assessment:</h3>\n\n\n\n<ol type="1"><li>Torba had no business raising public money at this stage in his development.</li><li>The balance sheet is thin, and almost non-existent.</li><li>There is no discussion of programming, or licensing or any R&amp;D activity; this is very odd for a technology company.</li><li>There is no discussion of his Christian priorities.</li><li>This is a marketing company, not a technology company.</li><li>There is no discussion of the plans to acquire or license the technology.</li><li>This \xe2\x80\x9cplan\xe2\x80\x9d appears to be a fake, a ruse, an excuse to feed Torba cash.</li><li>The money intermediary behind GAB is \xe2\x80\x9cStartEngine Capital, LLC\xe2\x80\x9d<ol type="a" start="1"><li><a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.startengine.com/" target="_blank">https://www.startengine.com/</a></li><li>Howard Marks, Co-founder; chairman of\xc2\xa0<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.activision.com/" target="_blank">Activision</a>\xc2\xa0Studios (gaming, $37 billion) sold to Disney; LA Mayor Garcetti\xe2\x80\x99s technology council. TRIPLE national: US, UK, France; <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.networkcomputing.com/networking/developers-disney-make-odd-couple-eclipsecon" target="_blank">Disney</a>\xc2\xa0and Activision are members of the IBM Eclipse Foundation, thief of social networking from Columbus, Ohio inventor Leader Technologies.</li><li>Ron Miller, Co-founder; WPO/YPO executive committee<br></li></ol></li></ol>\n\n\n\n<h2>Torba\xe2\x80\x99s tech guy, Andrew Cates, cut his teeth on IBM Eclipse Foundation social networking code stolen from Leader Technologies:\xc2\xa0Walmart, Netflix. href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Automate_Ads">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Automate_Ads</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Analysis of GAB</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">\n<span class="embed-youtube" style="text-align:center; display: block;"><iframe loading="lazy" class="youtube-player" width="845" height="476" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/iLsM014zb7E?version=3&#038;rel=1&#038;showsearch=0&#038;showinfo=1&#038;iv_load_policy=1&#038;fs=1&#038;hl=en-US&#038;autohide=2&#038;wmode=transparent" allowfullscreen="true" style="border:0;" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-presentation"></iframe></span>\n</div></figure>\n\n\n\n<p><a href="https://www.onenewspage.com/video/20220214/14337818/Andrew-Torba-aka-Robert-Torba-amp-Emily-Torba.htm">https://www.onenewspage.com/video/20220214/14337818/Andrew-Torba-aka-Robert-Torba-amp-Emily-Torba.htm</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p>In September 2017, Gab moved its headquarters to&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pennsylvania" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Pennsylvania</a>.<sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gab_(social_network)#cite_note-:5-238" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">[238]</a></sup>&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</a>&nbsp;(SEC) filings, as late as March 2018, stated that Torba operated Gab out of a&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WeWork" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">WeWork</a>&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coworking" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">coworking</a>&nbsp;space in&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philadelphia" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Philadelphia</a>.<sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gab_(social_network)#cite_note-WhatIsGab-239" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">[239]</a></sup>&nbsp;A WeWork spokesperson said that Torba had become a member under his own name, not Gab&#8217;s, and that his time there had been brief.<sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gab_(social_network)#cite_note-WhatIsGab-239" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">[239]</a></sup>&nbsp;In late October 2018, a Gab spokesperson told&nbsp;<em><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Philadelphia_Inquirer" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">The Philadelphia Inquirer</a></em>&nbsp;that Gab was no longer based in Philadelphia.<sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gab_(social_network)#cite_note-WhatIsGab-239" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">[239]</a></sup>&nbsp;As of January 2019, Gab is headquartered in&nbsp;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clarks_Summit,_Pennsylvania" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Clarks Summit, Pennsylvania</a>.<sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gab_(social_network)#cite_note-SEC_Filing-39" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">[39]</a></sup></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Andrew was raised in a middle class family and is the oldest of five children. His father&nbsp;Bob Torba, Jr&nbsp;has been a FedEx Express courier for 30+ years in the Pocono Mountains and recently retired to work full time for Gab. His mother&nbsp;Amy Torba&nbsp;was a stay-at-home mom for 25+ years and now lovingly dedicates her time helping animals at the local animal shelter.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Andrew is married to&nbsp;Emily Torba&nbsp;and is a loving father to their two children&nbsp;Sophia and Samuel.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<p><a href="https://www.ancestry.com/discoveryui-content/view/99780326:62209?tid=&amp;pid=&amp;queryId=4d7d84f143d6c9ace8a05a47ca6604b5&amp;_phsrc=pgH8&amp;_phstart=successSource">https://www.ancestry.com/discoveryui-content/view/99780326:62209?tid=&amp;pid=&amp;queryId=4d7d84f143d6c9ace8a05a47ca6604b5&amp;_phsrc=pgH8&amp;_phstart=successSource</a></p>\n\n\n\n<figure 2022</time></a></span>\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<a href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/05/12/von-reitz-v-mckibben-you-decide/" rel="permalink"><h1 class="entry-title">von Reitz v McKibben. You decide.</h1></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-header-column -->\n\t</div><!-- .entry-header-row -->\n</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class="entry-content">\n\t\n<p>We received this email from Anna von Reitz and share it with AIMCats so you could decide for yourself who Anna is.  We previously posted this piece which started this discussion between her and Michael. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2><a href="https://truthbits.blog/2022/03/04/not-interested-in-anna-von-reitz/"></a><a href="https://truthbits.blog/2022/03/04/not-interested-in-anna-von-reitz/">Why we are not interested in Anna von Reitz</a></h2>\n\n\n\n<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity"/>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>From:</strong>\xc2\xa0Anna von Reitz <br><strong>Sent:</strong>\xc2\xa0Monday, May 9, 2022 2:02 PM<br><strong>To:</strong>\xc2\xa0info@leader.com<br><strong>Subject:</strong>\xc2\xa0Attention: Mike McKibben About Court System, etc.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>My Compliments to Mike McKibben &#8212; and Leader Technologies</p>\n\n\n\n<p>[This is a response to Mike.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It is apparent that (1) Mike McKibben hasn\xe2\x80\x99t bothered to read what I have written to any appreciable extent \xe2\x80\x94 and is opening up his mouth anyway, or (2) is deliberately trying to misinform people.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>For example, my Readers know how often and how persistently I have said that the \xe2\x80\x9cBrits are at the bottom of the dogpile\xe2\x80\x9d and also know how often and how roundly I have criticized not only the Queen\xe2\x80\x99s Government, but the Lord Mayor\xe2\x80\x99s Government, too.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>A mere perusal of article titles would have given McKibben some grasp of my actual stance with regard to the British Raj, but he preferred his own (mistaken) presumptions over the facts. And didn\xe2\x80\x99t bother to look.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Other examples include the idea that I have ever advocated declaring oneself a \xe2\x80\x9cnatural person\xe2\x80\x9d \xe2\x80\x94 which is emphatically wrong; I have taught my Readers that \xe2\x80\x9cnatural person\xe2\x80\x9d is legalese for a corpse, literally, a dead body, and they should never accept or use any such description of themselves.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So again, McKibben presents false information which anyone can confirm by reading my articles on this subject.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Ditto the idea that I have ever claimed to be a Boston Brahmin, good or otherwise. My husband comes from a family that arrived in Boston in 1608 and played a major and honorable part in building and leading this country through the Revolution and for many years afterward.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>My point being that vilifying the founders of Boston is a grave disservice not only to those who gave so much to found this country and who shed their blood to set it free, but a gross disservice to history itself.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It\xe2\x80\x99s unlikely that there would have been an American Revolution without the Men of Boston and Massachusetts raising their objections to British tyranny.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Where did John and Samuel Adams\xe2\x80\x99 family hail from? Boston. Where was the Boston Tea Party? Boston. Where was the lantern that prompted Paul Revere\xe2\x80\x99s ride? Boston. Which port city endured the worst Naval Blockade in history up until that time\xe2\x80\x94 eight long years? Boston.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>McKibben obviously doesn\xe2\x80\x99t care much about me, about facts, or about history. He also seems rather slow on the uptake with his solution to his own problem.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If he bothered to read what I have been teaching people for years, he would know a great deal more about both the problem and his own proposed solution.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>For example, he would know that the Titles of Nobility Amendment ratified in 1819 and added to the actual Federal Constitution (1787) already prohibits Bar Attorneys from holding any public office in our American Government.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Nobody has to create that solution. We simply have to get organized, do our public duty, and enforce it.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Which is the \xe2\x80\x9crest of the story\xe2\x80\x9d McKibben does not\xe2\x80\x94 apparently\xe2\x80\x94 care to hear, because it puts the ultimate responsibility for correction on him and on all of us. Instead of beating his head against the stonewall of a King\xe2\x80\x99s Court and expecting justice from an institution created for completely different purposes (!) McKibben should stop whining about his stolen patents and ideas long enough to have a NEW thought.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And that thought would be that our own courts are missing, which leaves us at the mercy of the British Courts (which are here to pillage us).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If we would get organized and all properly declare ourselves Americans and form our courts (as many of us are doing) then we could all invoke Ex Parte Milligan (1866) and force these foreign courts to step down and leave us alone.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>We would finally have juries of our own peers again\xe2\x80\x94 American juries with no foreign allegiances and no axes to grind.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>McKibben has obviously suffered for lack of such a Court to hear his injuries and provide him with justice, but the simple fact that we must provide our own courts has sailed right over his head and the heads of literally millions of other Americans who have suffered at the hands of these foreign courts and apparently never wondered\xe2\x80\x94 where\xe2\x80\x99d my courts go?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Oh.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I have to gather my peers together.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>We have to declare that we are Americans, not Brits or whatever else.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>We have to assemble ourselves, hold our own elections, build our own jury pools, operate our own courts\xe2\x80\xa6.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>These same Angry Men, like McKibben, spend millions of dollars fighting the Papist and British Court Systems, year after year, but not ten cents toward building our own court system\xe2\x80\x94- the one thing that could and would give him and millions of others both justice and relief.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I\xe2\x80\x99m sorry, but if you keep making the same unexamined assumptions and doing the same things, you get the same results.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>How many YEARS has McKibben and Leader Technologies been in litigation over the invention of social media platforms \xe2\x80\x94 and gotten nothing but a huge attorney bill and a red nose to show for it?<br>Decades that I know of.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>McKibben has spent decades and probably millions of dollars looking for Justice in a foreign court.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But will he stop a moment and listen to a bit of history, realize how our American Courts almost disappeared \xe2\x80\x94- and move himself to solve that problem? So that he could then solve his own problem and everyone else\xe2\x80\x99s too\xe2\x80\x94- by reopening American Common Law Courts all over this country?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>He\xe2\x80\x99d rather spend his time trying to paint me as a disinformation agent and peeing on his own shoe, than take an oar and do what has to be done. He\xe2\x80\x99d rather bitch about foreign courts than build his own\xe2\x80\x94- then stand there like a Dumb Ox wondering why he can\xe2\x80\x99t get justice from a British Court against a British Corporation?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Please. I happen to sympathize with Leader Technologies. I happen to believe that McKibben was the inventor just as he says he was. And he got ripped off, too.<br>However, he is barking up the wrong tree.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>He can never get justice from a British Court and he apparently doesn\xe2\x80\x99t have sense enough to weigh in with me and build his own.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You are getting this reply from \xe2\x80\x9cAnna von Fritz\xe2\x80\x9d which is the name of my iPhone\xe2\x80\x94 but every letter has been pecked out on a tiny screen by my weary index finger.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Please return my compliments to Mike McKibben.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Anna Maria Riezinger, Fiduciary</p>\n\n\n\n<p>C/O Box 52&#8212;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Big Lake, href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/04/19/go-after-corrupt-school-board-go-after-their-bonds/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-04-19T15:12:13+00:00">April 19, 2022</time></a></span>\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<a href="https://patriots4truth.org/2022/04/19/go-after-corrupt-school-board-go-after-their-bonds/" rel="permalink"><h1 class="entry-title">Go after corrupt school board; Go after their bonds</h1></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-header-column -->\n\t</div><!-- .entry-header-row -->\n</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class="entry-content">\n\t\n<h3>Stop The Tyranny Fight Back</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>(Excerpt from <a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/stop-the-tyranny-fight-back/" rel="nofollow">https://bondsforthewin.com/stop-the-tyranny-fight-back/</a>)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>&#8220;Every Government Elected Official since 1792 is obligated to obtain a PUBLIC OFFICIAL SURETY bond before he can take the oath of office.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So why is this important to us?</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>The surety bond is a PERSONAL LIABLILITY to the Public Official.</li><li>The bond is our SECURITY and PERSONAL GUARANTEE that the Public Official will do his job and doesn\xe2\x80\x99t harm WE THE PEOPLE.</li><li>The Public Official has taken an oath to uphold the constitution of his state and of the United States.</li><li>If he fails to uphold the constitution, he is personally liable for all damages he has caused.</li><li>The surety bond is a two way contract between the Public Official and We The People.</li><li>If the Public Official breaks this contract We the People can file a claim against him personally through the Surety Bond Company.</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<p>Every action a Public Official does while he holds this office, he is personally responsible for. If he fails to uphold the constitution or enforces unlawful laws on We the People we can hold him personally accountable for these actions.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The Constitution of the United State, of each State and the Bill of Rights protects We the People. If enough people are tired of</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>Vaccine mandates</li><li>Mask mandate</li><li>Lockdowns</li><li>Business closures</li><li>Discrimination from businesses if we are not vaccinated</li><li>Forced mask mandates in public school</li><li>Forced vaccine mandates in businesses</li><li>Forced PCR testing to keep your job</li><li>Trying to force vaccines in public school</li><li>Critical race theory</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<p>We have the means to stop this now. Once we file a letter of intent to file a claim against the Public Officials surety bond he stands up and take notice. All it takes is 10 strong people to stand up and fight back. The Public Official is personally liable for each and every claim that is filed against their Surety Bond. He only has two choices now. Listen to our demands and change or pay us the full amount of his surety bond.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Once enough claims are filed against the surety bond the bond company will cancel his bond. This does not affect us. We will still be paid for all damages. If the Public Official surety bond is cancelled and he cannot obtain a new surety bond he is forced to step down. The Public Official cannot hold office if he cannot be bonded.&#8221;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>VIDEO <a href="https://www.bitchute.com/video/0rR4IGDMSGf6/">Go after the School Board, Go after their bonds &#8211; Bonds for the Win &#8211; Step 1: Obtain the Bond</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p>VIDEO <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.bitchute.com/video/WEFzrqoHtQsP/" target="_blank">Go after the School Board, Go after their bonds-Bonds for the Win &#8211; Step 2: Serve a Letter of Intent</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p>VIDEO <a href="https://www.bitchute.com/video/XQ9rpZUSr3g8/">Go after the School Board, Go after their bonds &#8211; Bonds for the Win &#8211; Step 3: Filing a Claim</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>(Excerpt from <a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/what-are-surety-bonds/" rel="nofollow">https://bondsforthewin.com/what-are-surety-bonds/</a>)</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>&#8220;The Public Official is NOT performing their duties for the community or they are enforcing mandates that are NOT laws upon the people.\xc2\xa0</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>ANYONE CAN:</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>Write a&nbsp;<a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/bond-request-letter-examples?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><strong>letter to the Public Official</strong></a>&nbsp;demanding a certified copy of their Surety Bond \xe2\x80\x93 every Public Official is required to provide this information by law.&nbsp; In some states you might be required to pay a small fee to obtain this copy.&nbsp;&nbsp;<br></li><li>Write a&nbsp;<strong><a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/intent-to-file-claim?swcfpc=1" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">letter to the Public Official</a></strong>&nbsp;of intent to file against the Surety Bond.&nbsp; State in this letter what harm he/she has caused you or the community, what needs to be done to rectify the situation, and the timeline for rectification.&nbsp; You should also include the amount of money they will be liable for and an explanation of how Surety Bonds work.&nbsp;<br></li><li>If the Public Official does not stop or take the action(s) you request, you can put them on notice by submitting a \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/2022/01/02/abuse-of-power-color-of-law-or-color-of-office" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><strong>Color of Law</strong></a>\xe2\x80\x9d violation.&nbsp;<br></li><li>If this fails, you can write a claim against the Public Official\xe2\x80\x99s Surety Bond.&nbsp; Depending on the laws of your state, more than one claim can be filed against a single bond holder.&nbsp; To submit this claim, simply write a letter to the company that holds the Surety Bond. State in this claim letter what harm the Public Official has caused you or the community. In some states the bonding company may require that you fill out a form.&nbsp;<br></li></ol>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>What Happens Next?</strong> </h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you file the claim the Bond Company will inform the Public Official.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>The Surety Company will then REQUIRE the Public Official to take care of the claim.<br></li><li>If the Public Official fails to take care of the claim the Surety Company will start an investigation to determine the claim\xe2\x80\x99s validity.<br></li><li>If the Surety Company determines your claim is invalid no further actions will be taken. The Public Official will be liable for any costs the Surety company incurred during the investigation process.<br></li><li>If the claim is valid the company will contact the Public Official and remind them of their obligations under the bond. The Public Official can either:<br>&nbsp;<ol><li>Offer a resolution to the claim which will include compensating YOU for any financial loss or damages incurred.<br>&nbsp; &nbsp; -OR-</li><li>They can submit a defense to the claim.&nbsp;</li></ol></li><li>If the Public Official fails to respond or resolve the claim the Surety Company will make a decision based upon the information and documentation that you provided for the claim. The Surety Company will then pay YOU for the claim.&nbsp; Once the Surety Company pays the claim they will go after the Public Official to reimburse the amount of the settlement and any legal costs associated with it.&nbsp;</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>Do We Have to Go To Court?</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>No, there is no need to go to court once you file a claim with the surety company. The surety company handles the claim and if needed, they will investigate the claim and pay you the damages. The Public Official is liable for all costs and the amount of the claim. Your claim cannot exceed the amount that is listed on the Surety Bond.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Keep in mind that once a claim is made, this does not immediately cancel the Surety Bond for the Public Official.&nbsp; According to the revised code of each state, more than one claim can be filed against a Public Official surety bond.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>What Happens to the Public Official?</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>This depends on the Surety Bond Company. If there are too many complaints made against the bond or too many claims paid out they might cancel the bond. Once a bond has been cancelled it will be difficult for the Public Official to be bonded or licenced again by any other Surety Bond Company.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Public Officials are required by law to be bonded in order to hold office. If their bond has been cancelled and they are unable to obtain a new bond they will not be able to hold any public office.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>How Does this Work in Our Favor?</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>If a Public Official is not performing his elected duties, these Surey Bonds give you, the public a chance to unseat them. This is one of the oldest laws on the books and it has been in effect since 1792.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The bond is a guarantee to We The People that Public Officials will not step outside the bounds of their office and enforce unlawful restrictions and laws on the public.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>Does This Also Work for Businesses?</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>There are many types of surety bonds. The type of business will determine the type of bond the business must carry. Remember you can always request a copy of the company\xe2\x80\x99s surety bond and read the provisions of the bond. Furthermore, there are different ways to file against other bonds and the surety bond company will supply you with this information upon request.&nbsp;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Note: In order to obtain and qualify for government contracts, employers must be licensed and bonded.\xc2\xa0 Generally the amount of coverage is based on the amount of the contract with the government.&#8221;</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity"/>\n\n\n\n<h2 class="has-text-align-center">LEARN MORE AND CALL TO ACTION. <a href="https://bondsforthewin.com/"
